 New Delhi: Sahitya Akademi organized a two-day seminar on the topic 'fine Essay: Format and Tradition'
 jiske udghaatan satr kii adhyakshata sahitya academy ke upaadhyaksh madhav kowshik ne kii or aarambhik vaktavy hindi paraamarsh mandal ke sanyojak chittaranjan mishra ne diya
 The opening statement was by Shyam Sundar Dubey and the seed statement was presented by Shriram Parihar
 swaagat bhaashan main sahitya academy ke sachiv ke
 Describing the characteristics of the Fine Essay, Srinivasrao said that a proper combination of words and expressions is necessary for a Fine Essay
 iske liye khaas tarah kii ekaagratha or nipunata kii aavashyaktaa hoti he
 That is why it is one of the most difficult genres of Hindi literature
 prakhyat samalochak chittaranjan mishra ne kaha ki lalit niabandh aatma kii abhivyakti he
 It can also be said that trying to convey the voice of your soul to another is a fine essay
 lalit niabandh aatma kii khabar he
 Hence it is also called self-expression essay
 lalit niabandh kii utkrushtataa, gyaan or anubhav ke saamanjasy par nirbhar karti he
 Mishra said that folk elements contain all things, in the same way all elements of literature are included in fine essays
 arthath lalit niabandh sahitya main lok tatva kaa sabase bada ashrayadata he
 Eminent Hindi writer Shyamsunder Dubey in the opening statement while discussing the challenges facing the Fine Essay said that no genre of Hindi literature would have faced such obstacles
 unhone lalit niabandh kii lokapriyata ke sandarbh main samarthyashalee pathakon kii charchaa kii
 He further said that in spite of so many questions and doubts, if a fine essay is developing, then it is a proof of its vitality and ability
 lok or shaastra kii jugalbandi hi achche lalit niabandh kii prishthbhumi hoti he or lalit niabandh pathakon ko bhashaayi drushti se samrudh banane kii prakriya he
 He also clarified that the ability to relate eternal memories is only in the Fine Essay
 prakhyat hindi lekhak shriram parihaar ne apane beej vaktavy main lalit niabandh kii vistrut paribhaasha dete hue kaha ki shaastra or srijan ke bich viksit vidha hi lalit niabandh he
 The Fine Essay follows the cyclical condition of the period and has a wide range of life
 arthath bhav or vichaar ke udvaig ko ramya bhashaa main prakat karne vaali vidha hi lalit niabandh he
 In his presidential statement, Madhav Kaushik, vice-president of Sahitya Akademi, said that Fine is doing the work of presenting our cultural dignity in today's downtrodden society
 lalit niabandh ne sahitya ko pathneey banane main mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaai he
 The first session of the symposium focused on the theme 'living the Fine Essay in the Essay Complex', which was chaired by Anant Mishra and Krishna Kumar Singh and Kaladhar Arya presented their articles
 krishna kumaar singh ne apane aalekh main kaha ki lok or paanditya main saamanjasy zaruri he tabhi lalit niabandh grahya honge
 Kaladhar Arya, while discussing the style of fine essays, while mentioning the contribution of writers of this tradition in Gujarati - Umashankar Joshi, Kaka Kalekar, etc
, said that in these essays, the essence of sentiment has been essential
 satr ke adhyaksh anant mishra ne kaha ki hamaari drushti kaa ksharan hota ja rahaa he or isiilie lalit niabandh lekhan kam hota ja rahaa he
 Marketist, consumerist, contradictory times have affected our sensitivity and because of this we are not able to give time to the fine essay in totality
 is kaarykram kaa dwitiya satr ‘lalit niabandh kaa saanskrithik parisar’ par kendrit tha, jisaki adhyakshata chittaranjan mishra ne kii or indushekhar tatpurush evam shriram parihaar ne aalekh-paath kiya
 Indushekhar Tatpurush discussed in detail the various aspects of culture and their political discussions
 unhone ramdhaari singh ‘dinakar’ or namvar singh ke likhit nibandhon se kai udhaaharan prastut kiye
 Sri Ram Parihar considered the Fine Essay to be a purely Indian genre and said that its references are available in our very old Sanskrit literature
 bhartiya samskruti ke paanch tattvon kaa zikr karte hue unhone kaha ki bhartiya lalit niabandh ne vibhinn sabhyataaon or paramparaon ko apane saath liya he or ek apni samgr saanskrithik drushti viksit kii he
 The president of the session, Chittaranjan Mishra, said that the Fine Essay reconsiders the nature of culture and also records the decline in culture
 unhone shaastra or lok kii tulana karte hue kaha ki donon main dwandv hona chahie tabhi swasth samskritiyon kaa vikaas hota he
 The program was moderated by Sahitya Akademi editor Anupam Tiwari
 kaarykram main badi sankhya main sahitya premi upasthit rahe
 The next day sessions on 'lalit Essay Tradition: Purvarang' and 'lalit Essay Tradition: Uttar Rang' are held

 The Master of Business Management, ie MBA is a 2-year course in which students are made expert in all subjects of management and are made experts of one subject
 emb ke pehle saal main students kaa parichay management se jude tamaam subjects se karaayaa jaataa he
 After this, information about specialized subjects is also given
 emb ke duusare saal main studentrus ko apni pasand ke kisi ek speshlined subject ko chunanaa hota he
 This does not apply to students who have taken admission in a specialized course (sectoral MBA)
 studentrus ke liye speshlined course chunanaa ek kathin prakriya he
 Students should take special care of their career goals and professional development before choosing specialization
 yahaan par ham aapako emb kii top 10 streems ke bare main bataa rahe hai:(1) finans:emb in finans emb speshligeshan kaa sabase purana subject he
 During this course you are prepared for subjects such as costing, budgeting, international finance and capital management
 in subjects kii padhai karne ke baad aap finantial management main speshlined ban jate hai, jisase aapako kisi bhi orgenigeshan ke finans department main job mil sakati he
 If you want to do MBA in Finance then you should be a graduate in any stream
 (2) marketing:emb marketing dianemic or kaaphi compatitive he
 MBA marketing helps students understand consumer behavior, markets, advertising and other specifics related to this field
 is field main un logon ko kariyar bananaa chahie jinaki communication skills behtareen hon, maujuuda risource kaa sahi tareeke se istemaal karne kii kala aati ho or marketing main tike rahanaa kaa jajba ho
 (3) Human Resource (HR): MBA in HR is for those who want to pursue a career in HR and Strategy
 acchhee communication skills, aakarshak persenality or aatmavishvasi vaale logon ke liye echaar main emb ek acha kariyar opshan he
 Graduates in any stream can do MBA in HR

 This MBA degree focuses more on multinational cooperation
 is course main admician ke liye kisi bhi stream se graduate hona jaruri he
 (5) Operations: MBA in operations is helpful in production management or shop floor management
 is course ke jariye aap process flo ko mentin karnaa ke alaava vendor or inter-departmental relations ko banaae rakhane kaa gun sikhte hai
 Most of the students in engineering background do MBA in Operations as they do not have much difficulty in getting into this field due to knowledge of product development, designing and process optimization
 haalanki kisi bhi stream ke ummidavaar is course ke liye aplai kar sakate hai
 (6) Information Technology (IT): The MBA in IT is designed to prepare professionals who can effectively manage planning, design, selection, implementation and administration related to information and communication technology
 bijness team main iti graduates ek mahatvapurn bhoomika adaa karte hai
 Especially in designing and implementation of software solutions
 kisi bhi stream ke ummidavaar iti main emb kar sakate hai
 (7) Supply Chain Management: Under this course information about inventory management, warehousing and clients or transportation of all types of materials demanded by a company is given
 supplai chen management main kisi bhi stream ke grajuts emb kar sakate hai
 (8) Rural Management: MBA in Rural Management is a unique program designed to meet the growing demand of skill managers in the field of Rural Business Marketing
 rural market main vikaas kii sambhaavnaaen bahut zyada hai or korporate gharaanon ko is baat kaa acchhee tarah ehsaas he

 Keeping in mind the special needs of the agribusiness sector, students should have a good understanding of management, marketing and finance

" " lekin gauda abhi kuch karte, uske pehle hi lagbhag chah maheene main 10 november, 2014 ko railway ke kayakalp kii jimmedaari suresh prabhu ko saunp di gai

 iske liye paise kii jarurat bataakar safar mahangaa kiya gaya

 phir, 3 sitambar, 2017 ko piyush goyal ko rail mahakme kii jimmedaari di gai
 Neither the accident stopped, nor a special initiative to fix security was seen
 lihaaja, modi sarkaar ke lagbhag 44 maheene ke kaarykaal main ab tak kul 27 train durghatana main 259 log maare gaye or 899 ghayal hue
 That is, every two months 1 railway accident occurred

 48 lakh crore Rs

 sangraksha kaa fund alag-alag vibhaagon main kharch hota he

 magar kodh main khaaj yah ki in vibhaagon ke rakhwalon main koi talmail nahin hota
 However, how strong coordination is required between them, it can be understood from this that if the maintenance of rolling stock is good but the maintenance of the tracks is not good then the rail traffic is not safe
 isliye sangraksha main ekarupata jaruri he
 This means that a separate department is necessary for fullproof safety
 sangraksha main doosraa chhed is mad main staff kii baari kami he
 7,46,676 employees are engaged in railway safety work
 inamen gangamain, getman vagairah shaamil hai

 patariyon main padane vaale crack, fish plate kii khamiyaan or todfod jaisi samasyaon ko dur karne ke liye in staff kii jarurat he
 Minister of State for Railways Manoj Sinha says, "there is a continuous work in the railways regarding safety
 khaali padon ko bharne kaa kaam chal rahaa he

 is bajet main railway ko pehle ke mukaable 3 guna adhik fund mila he jo sangraksha or aadhunikeekaran par kharch hoga
 “but perches are many
 railway ke aadhunikeekaran or sangraksha ko lekar bajet praavdhaan ko thik-thaak maan liya jaae to bhi yah sawaal uthta he ki koi time frem kyon tay nahin kiya gaya he? is par railway board ke adhikariyon kaa kahana he ki in kaaryon ke liye time frem tay nahin kiya ja saktaa

 adhikariyon kaa kahana he ki 63,000 kilometre kii rail line 1,219 section se guzarati he

 yani lagbhag 42,000 kilometre trek par trephic lod apane charam par he
 Freight trains also run on the same track, superfast and local trains like rajdhani-shatabdi also run
 aise main trainon kaa samay se parichaalan or sangraksha ke saath parichaalan kaaphi kathin he

 Officials claim that the construction of a dedicated freight corridor for the movement of goods trains is going on fast
 yah kaam puraa hote hi rail patariyon par yatayaat kaa dabaav kam hoga

 is baar bhi 1
